HOW TO USE THIS PRICE LIST
1. Printed versions of this price list are for reference only. Please visit www.trimcohardware.com for the most recent revision.
2. Pricing is as indicated for standard finishes. 605, 613, 613E, 622, 316P, 316S, 625, 626, 628, 629, and 630. Additional
finishes are available as shown below. If a price is not shown for a particular finish, it may be available at the special
price or by special quotation if quantaties warrant. Minimum quantities may apply.
3. As a matter of convenience, those items commonly stocked are marked with a box surrounding the price. We will attempt
to have the boxed items in-stock.
4. Items formerly offered, but not in this price list may be available by special order and quotation only, provided basic
materials & tooling are available.
5. When ordering, please use numbers and finishes as indicated in price list. It will expedite the entering of your order, and
reduce the chance of error due to incorrect interpretation.
6. Some products are marked with the following logos:
Products with a UL listing.
Products that meet ADA and/or Barrier Free requirements.
Products that can be manufactured with Healthy Hardware bactericidal copper alloys.
